\put(73.263,-88.07202){\fontsize{11}{1}\usefont{T1}{ptm}{m}{it}\selectfont\color{color_29791} Waste Management are minimization of domestic, medical, hazardous, and non-hazardous}
\put(55.85,-102.563){\fontsize{11}{1}\usefont{T1}{ptm}{m}{it}\selectfont\color{color_29791}wastes, separate collection at the source, intermediate storage, establishment of transfer centers for}
\put(55.85,-117.054){\fontsize{11}{1}\usefont{T1}{ptm}{m}{it}\selectfont\color{color_29791}wastes when necessary, transportation, recovery, disposal of wastes, operation of recovery and}
\put(55.85,-131.545){\fontsize{11}{1}\usefont{T1}{ptm}{m}{it}\selectfont\color{color_29791}disposal facilities, closure, post-closure maintenance, it is a management style that includes }

\put(73.263,-168.527){\fontsize{11}{1}\usefont{T1}{ptm}{m}{it}\selectfont\color{color_29791} The basic policy is to reduce the amount of waste, recycle waste, reuse, and recycle as an energy }
\put(55.85,-183.0181){\fontsize{11}{1}\usefont{T1}{ptm}{m}{it}\selectfont\color{color_29791}source}
\put(73.263,-205.509){\fontsize{11}{1}\usefont{T1}{ptm}{m}{it}\selectfont\color{color_29791} In Waste Management, we have a hierarchy.}
\put(73.263,-384.141){\fontsize{11}{1}\usefont{T1}{ptm}{m}{it}\selectfont\color{color_29791} In the world where billions of people live, waste is produced as a result of every product it}
\put(55.85,-398.632){\fontsize{11}{1}\usefont{T1}{ptm}{m}{it}\selectfont\color{color_29791}produces in order to raise the living standards of people. These wastes can pose a serious health}
\put(55.85,-413.123){\fontsize{11}{1}\usefont{T1}{ptm}{m}{it}\selectfont\color{color_29791}issues if not managed properly. Moreover, we need to manage these wastes correctly in order to}
\put(55.85,-427.614){\fontsize{11}{1}\usefont{T1}{ptm}{m}{it}\selectfont\color{color_29791}protect our world because of the fact that if we do not have an optimized waste management system,}
\put(55.85,-442.105){\fontsize{11}{1}\usefont{T1}{ptm}{m}{it}\selectfont\color{color_29791}the methane gas (CH4) emitted by the garbage primarily affects the global warming in our world, but }
\put(55.85,-456.596){\fontsize{11}{1}\usefont{T1}{ptm}{m}{it}\selectfont\color{color_29791}in addition to these effects, it has many damages.}
